│  > ⸻                                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                    │
│    **For Gemini: Fix Broken Python (pyenv “Undefined error: 0”/Silent Failures)**                                                  │
│    ```bash                                                                                                                         │
│    # Gemini, do the following to fix the Python silent failure in pyenv:                                                           │
│    ## 1. Remove and Reinstall the Broken Python Version:                                                                           │
│        pyenv uninstall 3.11.9 || true                                                                                              │
│        pyenv install 3.11.9                                                                                                        │
│        pyenv rehash                                                                                                                │
│    ## 2. Confirm Python is Working:                                                                                                │
│        ~/.pyenv/versions/3.11.9/bin/python -c "print('PYTHON_OK')"                                                                 │
│    ## 3. If you still see errors or no output, try using the Homebrew Python instead:                                              │
│        brew install python@3.11                                                                                                    │
│        /opt/homebrew/bin/python3.11 -c "print('BREW_PYTHON_OK')"                                                                   │
│    ## 4. If Homebrew Python works, set it as default (or use it explicitly for pip/test runs).                                     │
│    # How to handle ongoing failures:                                                                                               │
│    # - If all pythons are failing, check 'xcode-select --install' and re-run installs.                                             │
│    # - Always prefer Homebrew Python on Apple Silicon (ARM) if pyenv keeps failing.                                                │
│    # - If you see "Undefined error: 0" or zero output for any 'python -c' call, the interpreter is corrupted; reinstall as above.  │
│    # - If you must automate, wrap all Python calls with a quick output check and error report.                                     │
│    # Optional: Wipe pyenv cache (in case of persistent build failures):                                                            │
│        rm -rf ~/.pyenv/cache                                                                                                       │
│    ```                                                                                                                             │
│                                                                                                                                    │
│    ⸻                                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                    │
│    **Explanation for Non-Humans (Gemini, Agent, etc):**                                                                            │
│    ```md                                                                                                                           │
│    •If the command python -c "print('something')" returns nothing, that Python is broken.                                          │
│    •Always uninstall and reinstall the version first (pyenv uninstall/install).                                                    │
│    •If using Homebrew Python, always use the full path (/opt/homebrew/bin/python3.11).                                             │
│    •If *all* installs fail, make sure macOS CLI tools are up to date with xcode-select --install.                                  │
│    •**Never** keep retrying a broken interpreter—reinstall or swap to a known-good binary.                                         │
│    ```                                                                                                                             │
│    ⸻                                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                    │
│    **One-Liner Health Check**                                                                                                      │
│                                                                                                                                    │
│    ```bash                                                                                                                         │
│    ~/.pyenv/versions/3.11.9/bin/python -c "print('OK')" || /opt/homebrew/bin/python3.11 -c "print('OK')"                           │
│    ```                                                                                                                             │
│                                                                                                                                    │
│    ⸻                                                                                                                               │
│                                                                                                                                    │
│    This is the “hit it with a hammer” way to make it work, every time.                                                             │
│                                                                                                                                    │
│    **This will fix the vast majority of “silent Python fails” under Gemini, pyenv, or any CI/CD runner on macOS.**                 │

 ╭────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
 │ ✔ ReadFile ...valy-Agentic-FayeBlade/backend/main.py  │
 ╰────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
✦ I've reviewed backend/main.py and found several critical issues.

  Security Vulnerabilities:
   * CORS: Wide-open CORS policy.
   * Authentication: No authentication on any endpoint.
   * Hardcoded URLs: The agent URL is hardcoded.
   * Error Handling: Leaks internal details.
   * Path Traversal: Potential vulnerability in get_attack_data.
   * RCE: The tool_call endpoint is a critical remote code execution vulnerability.

  Code Quality Issues:
   * Hardcoded User: The username is hardcoded in create_session.
   * Brittle Report Handling: Relies on regex to find report files.
   * `sys.path` Manipulation: Unsafe sys.path modification.

  My Plan:
   1. Remove the `tool_call` endpoint immediately to patch the RCE vulnerability.
   2. Implement simple API key authentication.
   3. Make CORS and the agent URL configurable via environment variables.
   4. Add a path traversal check to get_attack_data.
   5. Remove the hardcoded username.
   6. Flag the regex report handling as a minor bug for later.

  I'll start by removing the tool_call endpoint. I'll read the file content first to ensure a precise replacement.
